Bootstrap Policy Verb Sets** (`plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/policy.go:37-40`)\\n- `Write = []string{\\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\"}`\\n- `ReadWrite = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\"}`\\n- `Read = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\"}`\\n- `ReadUpdate = []string{\\\"get\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\"}`\\n\\nThese constants serve as the standard verb groupings used throughout the RBAC authorization system to define permissions for different controller roles.\\n\\n**2. Verb Mapping for Discovery** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go:177-189`)\\nThe `toDiscoveryKubeVerb` map translates internal HTTP verbs to canonical kube verbs:\\n- POST → create\\n- PUT → update\\n- GET → get\\n- DELETE → delete\\n- PATCH → patch\\n- LIST → list\\n- WATCH → watch\\n- DELETECOLLECTION → deletecollection\\n- WATCHLIST → watch\\n- CONNECT → (not listed in discovery)\\n\\n**3. Request Processing Verb Classification** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/request/requestinfo.go:76-90`)\\n- `specialVerbs = sets.NewString(\\\"proxy\\\", \\\"watch\\\")`\\n- `verbsWithSelectors = sets.NewString(\\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\")` - These verbs support fieldSelector and labelSelector parameters\\n\\n**4. CLI Verb Validation** (`staging/src/k8s.io/kubectl/pkg/cmd/create/create_role.go:60`)\\n- `validResourceVerbs = []string{\\\"*\\\", \\\"get\\\", \\\"delete\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"update\\\", \\\"patch\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"proxy\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\", \\\"use\\\", \\\"bind\\\", \\\"escalate\\\", \\\"impersonate\\\"}`\\n\\n### API Handler Implementation Chain\\n\\n**Endpoint Installation** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`)\\nThe API installer registers handlers for each verb by examining storage interfaces and creating routes:\\n- Routes based on REST verb detection (GET, POST, PUT, PATCH, DELETE)\\n- APIResource objects created with Verbs field populated from supported storage operations\\n- Handler registration via `restful` web service framework\\n\\n**Handler Implementations** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/`)\\n- `get.go`: GetResource() - implements \\\"get\\\" verb via Getter interface\\n- `create.go`: CreateResource() - implements \\\"create\\\" verb via Creater interface  \\n- `update.go`: UpdateResource() - implements \\\"update\\\" verb via Updater interface\\n- `patch.go`: PatchResource() - implements \\\"patch\\\" verb via Patcher interface\\n- `delete.go`: DeleteResource() and DeleteCollection() - implements \\\"delete\\\" and \\\"deletecollection\\\" verbs\\n- `watch.go`: ListResource() with forceWatch parameter - implements \\\"list\\\" and \\\"watch\\\" verbs\\n\\n**Storage Interface Definitions** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/rest.go`)\\nREAL storage backend implementations must satisfy these interfaces to support verbs:\\n- Getter - for GET (get)\\n- Creater - for POST (create)\\n- Updater - for PUT (update)\\n- Deleter/GracefulDeleter - for DELETE (delete)\\n- CollectionDeleter - for DELETECOLLECTION (deletecollection)\\n- Lister - for GET with no name (list)\\n- Watcher - for WATCH (watch)\\n- Patcher - for PATCH (patch)\\n\\n### RBAC Authorization Enforcement\\n\\n**Authorization Decision** (`plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go`)\\n- RBACAuthorizer.Authorize() method checks if request verb matches PolicyRule.Verbs\\n- Uses VerbMatches() helper for matching logic\\n\\n**Verb Matching Logic** (`pkg/apis/rbac/v1/evaluation_helpers.go:26-35`)\\n```go\\nfunc VerbMatches(rule *rbacv1.PolicyRule, requestedVerb string) bool {\\n  for _, ruleVerb := range rule.Verbs {\\n    if ruleVerb == rbacv1.VerbAll { // \\\"*\\\" matches all verbs\\n      return true\\n    }\\n    if ruleVerb == requestedVerb {\\n      return true\\n    }\\n  }\\n  return false\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Verb Validation for ResourceNames** (`pkg/apis/rbac/helpers.go:186-196`)\\nWhen ResourceNames are specified, certain verbs are not allowed:\\n- \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"create\\\", \\\"deletecollection\\\" are blacklisted with ResourceNames\\n- This prevents invalid authorization rules\\n\\n**Policy Rule Breakdown** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-helpers/auth/rbac/validation/policy_comparator.go:56-71`)\\nBreakdownRule() decomposes complex rules into atomic verbs for comparison and validation\\n\\n### API Discovery and Resource Verb Exposure\\n\\n**APIResource Verb Field** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1/types.go:1203-1205`)\\nEvery APIResource object includes:\\n```\\nVerbs: []string // list of supported kube verbs (get, list, watch, create, update, patch, delete, deletecollection, proxy)\\n```\\n\\n**Discovery Helper** (`staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/discovery/helper.go:138-146`)\\n- SupportsAllVerbs predicate filters resources by required verbs\\n- Used by quota controller: GetQuotableResources filters for resources supporting [\\\"create\\\", \\\"list\\\", \\\"watch\\\", \\\"delete\\\"]\\n\\n**APIResourceDiscovery Types** (`staging/src/k8s.io/api/apidiscovery/v2/types.go`, `pkg/apis/apidiscovery/types.go`)\\nStructured discovery objects that include Verbs arrays for aggregated discovery endpoint\\n\\n### Custom Resource Verb Handling\\n\\n**CRD Discovery** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_discovery_controller.go`)\\n- Builds verb lists from CRD spec.versions[].served and storage.storageClusters\\n- Populates APIResource.Verbs for custom resources\\n\\n**CRD Handler Routes** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go:371-425`)\\n- Router switches on verb string to route to appropriate handler\\n- Supports: get, list, watch, create, update, patch, delete, deletecollection\\n\\n### Summary of Verb Coverage\\n\\nAll 8 standard verbs are comprehensively implemented:\\n1. **get** - Single resource retrieval via Getter interface and GetResource handler\\n2. **list** - Collection retrieval via Lister interface and ListResource handler  \\n3. **watch** - Streaming changes via Watcher interface and ListResource handler with forceWatch=true\\n4. **create** - Resource creation via Creater interface and CreateResource handler\\n5. **update** - Full resource replacement via Updater interface and UpdateResource handler\\n6. **patch** - Partial resource updates via Patcher interface and PatchResource handler\\n7. **delete** - Single resource deletion via GracefulDeleter interface and DeleteResource handler\\n8. **deletecollection** - Collection deletion via CollectionDeleter interface and DeleteCollection handler\\n\\nEach verb is:\\n- Defined as a string constant and grouped in bootstrap policies\\n- Mapped from HTTP methods in the discovery system\\n- Implemented via specific storage interfaces that backends must satisfy\\n- Enforced by RBAC authorization rules with matching logic\\n- Exposed in API discovery for clients to discover supported operations\\n- Validated in RBAC rules to prevent invalid
